on note{thread-unsafe}
	ignore_event(EVENT_ID{int}){Builtin, None}
	set_key_pressed(EVENT_NOTE{int}, 1){Builtin, None}
		keyswitches_on_note(EVENT_NOTE{int}, group_count000{int}, v00{int}, idx000000{int}){UserDefined, ParameterStack}

	if(pressed_keys[EVENT_NOTE{int}]{int} = - 1)
		pressed_keys[EVENT_NOTE{int}]{int} := ENGINE_UPTIME{int}
		last_pressed[EVENT_NOTE{int}]{int} := ENGINE_UPTIME{int}
		key_velocity[EVENT_NOTE{int}]{int} := EVENT_VELOCITY{int}
		inc(num_pressed_keys{int}){Builtin, None}
	end if
	last_on_note_callback{int} := NI_CALLBACK_ID{int}
		wait_or_zero(note_selection_time{int} * 1000){UserDefined, ParameterStack}

	if(last_on_note_callback{int} = NI_CALLBACK_ID{int})
			update_selected_notes(v00{int}, group_count000{int}, idx000000{int}, articulation_event_id000{int}, set_articulation_event_id000{int}, next_free_idx0000{int}, idx3000{int}, i1000{int}, is_free0000{int}, _ret110000{int}, result10000{int}){UserDefined, ParameterStack}

	end if
end on

on release{thread-unsafe}
	if(get_event_mark(EVENT_ID{int}, MARK_1{int}){Builtin, None} = FALSE{int})
		set_key_pressed(EVENT_NOTE{int}, 0){Builtin, None}
		last_release_callback{int} := NI_CALLBACK_ID{int}
		ignore_event(EVENT_ID{int}){Builtin, None}
		pressed_keys[EVENT_NOTE{int}]{int} := - 1
		dec(num_pressed_keys{int}){Builtin, None}
		if(sustain_pedal{int} = OFF{int})
			message("added note off event to queue"){Builtin, None}
				articulations_note_off(0, EVENT_NOTE{int}, idx000000{int}, group_count000{int}, v00{int}, articulation_event_id000{int}, set_articulation_event_id000{int}){UserDefined, ParameterStack}

				wait_or_zero(note_selection_time{int} * 1000){UserDefined, ParameterStack}

			if(last_release_callback{int} = NI_CALLBACK_ID{int})
					update_selected_notes(set_articulation_event_id000{int}, articulation_event_id000{int}, v00{int}, group_count000{int}, idx000000{int}, idx3000{int}, i1000{int}, next_free_idx0000{int}, is_free0000{int}, _ret110000{int}, result10000{int}){UserDefined, ParameterStack}

			end if
		end if
	end if
end on

on controller{thread-unsafe}
	ignore_controller{Builtin, None}
	controller_value0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{int} := CC[CC_NUM{int}]{int}
	if(CC_NUM{int} = 1)
			buffer_modwheel_animation(CC[1]{int}){UserDefined, ParameterStack}

		set_control_par(get_ui_id(sli_modwheel_slider{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, CC[1]{int}){Builtin, None}
	end if
	if(CC_NUM{int} = 64)
		if(CC[64]{int} > 63)
			sustain_pedal_actual{int} := ON{int}
		else
			sustain_pedal_actual{int} := OFF{int}
			sustain_pedal{int} := OFF{int}
			i{int} := 0
			while(i{int} <= 127) 
				if(pressed_keys[i{int}]{int} = - 1)
					ii{int} := 0
					while(ii{int} <= (NUM_INSTRUMENTS{int} - 1)) 
							articulations_note_off(ii{int}, i{int}, result10000{int}, _ret110000{int}, is_free0000{int}, next_free_idx0000{int}, i1000{int}){UserDefined, ParameterStack}

						inc(ii{int}){Builtin, None}
					end while
				end if
				inc(i{int}){Builtin, None}
			end while
		end if
	end if
		wait_or_zero(lookahead{int} * 1000){UserDefined, ParameterStack}

	sustain_pedal{int} := sustain_pedal_actual{int}
	if(CC_NUM{int} = 1)
			set_modulation_position(0, controller_value0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{int}){UserDefined, ParameterStack}

			cc_on_controller(i1000{int}, next_free_idx0000{int}, is_free0000{int}, _ret110000{int}, result10000{int}, idx3000{int}, idx000000{int}, group_count000{int}, v00{int}, articulation_event_id000{int}, subarticulation_modulation_strength000{real}, set_articulation_event_id000{int}, fade_in_range000{int}, fade_out_end000{int}, fade_out_range000{int}){UserDefined, ParameterStack}

	end if
end on

on listener
		delay_buffer_execute(set_articulation_event_id000{int}, articulation_event_id000{int}, v00{int}, group_count000{int}, idx000000{int}, idx3000{int}, subarticulation_modulation_strength000{real}, result10000{int}, _ret110000{int}, is_free0000{int}, next_free_idx0000{int}, i1000{int}, fade_out_end000{int}, fade_in_range000{int}, fade_out_range000{int}, start_note000{int}, end_note000{int}, transition_note000{int}, transition_type000{int}, transition_dyn_layer000{int}, _ret21000{int}, result6000{int}){UserDefined, ParameterStack}

	if((animation_frame_counter{int} = 0) and (next_modwheel_animation_frame{int} # - 1))
			set_background_animation(next_modwheel_animation_frame{int}){UserDefined, ParameterStack}

		if(get_control_par(get_ui_id(pnl_editor_page{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}){Builtin, None} = HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int})
				editor_update_modwheel_position(next_modwheel_animation_frame{int}){UserDefined, ParameterStack}

		end if
		next_modwheel_animation_frame{int} := - 1
	end if
	animation_frame_counter{int} := (animation_frame_counter{int} + 1) mod (ANIMATION_RESOLUTION{int} / LISTENER_RESOLUTION{int})
end on

	xy_modwheel_assignment[0 + 1]{real} := 1
	xy_modwheel_assignment[4 + 1]{real} := 1
	if(NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE{int} = NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE_LEFT_BUTTON_DOWN{int})
		if((get_control_par(get_ui_id(xy_modwheel_assignment{real[]}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_ACTIVE_INDEX{int}){Builtin, None} = 0) or (get_control_par(get_ui_id(xy_modwheel_assignment{real[]}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_ACTIVE_INDEX{int}){Builtin, None} = 4))
			set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_fade_circle_md{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int}){Builtin, None}
		end if
	else
		if(NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE{int} = NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE_LEFT_BUTTON_UP{int})
			set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_fade_circle_md{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{int}){Builtin, None}
		end if
	end if
	ma_cb_id{int} := NI_CALLBACK_ID{int}
	if((get_control_par(get_ui_id(xy_modwheel_assignment{real[]}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_ACTIVE_INDEX{int}){Builtin, None} = 2) and (xy_modwheel_assignment[2]{real} <= xy_modwheel_assignment[4]{real}))
		if(xy_modwheel_assignment[0]{real} < xy_modwheel_assignment[2]{real})
			xy_modwheel_assignment[0]{real} := xy_modwheel_assignment[2]{real}
		end if
		_loaded_subarticulations_start[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int} := int(xy_modwheel_assignment[2]{real} * 127){Builtin, None}
	else
		if(((get_control_par(get_ui_id(xy_modwheel_assignment{real[]}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_ACTIVE_INDEX{int}){Builtin, None} = 0) and (xy_modwheel_assignment[2]{real} <= xy_modwheel_assignment[0]{real})) and (xy_modwheel_assignment[2]{real} <= xy_modwheel_assignment[4]{real}))
			set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_fade_circle_md{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}, get_control_par(get_ui_id(xy_modwheel_assignment{real[]}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None} + int(xy_modwheel_assignment[0]{real} * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id(xy_modwheel_assignment{real[]}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH{int}){Builtin, None} - 20){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
			_loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int} := int(round((xy_modwheel_assignment[0]{real} - xy_modwheel_assignment[2]{real}) * 127){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
		else
			if(((get_control_par(get_ui_id(xy_modwheel_assignment{real[]}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_ACTIVE_INDEX{int}){Builtin, None} = 4) and (xy_modwheel_assignment[0]{real} <= xy_modwheel_assignment[4]{real})) and (xy_modwheel_assignment[4]{real} <= xy_modwheel_assignment[6]{real}))
				set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_fade_circle_md{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}, get_control_par(get_ui_id(xy_modwheel_assignment{real[]}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None} + int(xy_modwheel_assignment[4]{real} * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id(xy_modwheel_assignment{real[]}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH{int}){Builtin, None} - 20){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
				_loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int} := int((xy_modwheel_assignment[6]{real} - xy_modwheel_assignment[4]{real}) * 127){Builtin, None}
			else
				if((get_control_par(get_ui_id(xy_modwheel_assignment{real[]}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_ACTIVE_INDEX{int}){Builtin, None} = 6) and (xy_modwheel_assignment[0]{real} <= xy_modwheel_assignment[6]{real}))
					if(xy_modwheel_assignment[4]{real} > xy_modwheel_assignment[6]{real})
						xy_modwheel_assignment[4]{real} := xy_modwheel_assignment[6]{real}
					end if
					_loaded_subarticulations_end[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int} := int(xy_modwheel_assignment[6]{real} * 127){Builtin, None}
				end if
			end if
		end if
	end if
	wait(10000){Builtin, None}
	if(ma_cb_id{int} = NI_CALLBACK_ID{int})
			update_modwheel_assignment_control{UserDefined, Call}

			update_modwheel_assignment_circles{UserDefined, Call}

	end if
end on

on ui_control(xy_center_circles{real[]}){thread-unsafe}
	cc_cb_id{int} := NI_CALLBACK_ID{int}
	if(NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE{int} = NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE_LEFT_BUTTON_DOWN{int})
			center_circle_distance(distance0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real}, xy_center_circles[0]{real}, xy_center_circles[1]{real}, subarticulation_modulation_strength000{real}, dy00{real}){UserDefined, Inlining}

			center_circle_angle(angle1[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real}, xy_center_circles[0]{real}, xy_center_circles[1]{real}, subarticulation_modulation_strength000{real}, dy00{real}, cos_theta00{real}, angle00{real}){UserDefined, Inlining}

			angle_to_value(controller_value0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{int}, angle1[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real}, 0.7, (NI_MATH_PI{real} * 2) - 0.7, dy00{real}){UserDefined, ParameterStack}

		if((distance0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real} >= 0.32) and (distance0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real} < 0.36))
			selected_subarticulation{int} := 0
		else
			if((distance0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real} >= 0.36) and (distance0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real} < 0.4))
				selected_subarticulation{int} := 1
			else
				if((distance0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real} >= 0.4) and (distance0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real} < 0.44))
					selected_subarticulation{int} := 2
				else
					if((distance0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real} >= 0.44) and (distance0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real} < 0.48))
						selected_subarticulation{int} := 3
					end if
				end if
			end if
		end if
		if(abs(controller_value0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{int} - _loaded_subarticulations_start[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int}){Builtin, None} < 10)
			selected_circle_end{int} := 0
		else
			if(abs(controller_value0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{int} - _loaded_subarticulations_end[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int}){Builtin, None} < 10)
				selected_circle_end{int} := 1
			else
				selected_circle_end{int} := - 1
			end if
		end if
			update_subarticulation_selection(set_articulation_event_id000{int}){UserDefined, ParameterStack}

	end if
	if(NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE{int} = NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE_DRAG{int})
		wait(10000){Builtin, None}
		if((cc_cb_id{int} = NI_CALLBACK_ID{int}) and (selected_circle_end{int} # - 1))
				center_circle_angle(angle1[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real}, xy_center_circles[0]{real}, xy_center_circles[1]{real}, dy00{real}, subarticulation_modulation_strength000{real}, cos_theta00{real}, angle00{real}){UserDefined, Inlining}

				angle_to_value(controller_value0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{int}, angle1[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real}, 0.7, (NI_MATH_PI{real} * 2) - 0.7, angle00{real}){UserDefined, ParameterStack}

			if(selected_circle_end{int} = 0)
				if(controller_value0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{int} < ((_loaded_subarticulations_end[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int} - _loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int}) - _loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int}))
					_loaded_subarticulations_start[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int} := controller_value0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{int}
				end if
			else
				if(selected_circle_end{int} = 1)
					if(controller_value0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{int} > ((_loaded_subarticulations_start[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int} + _loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int}) + _loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int}))
						_loaded_subarticulations_end[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int} := controller_value0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{int}
					end if
				end if
			end if
				update_modwheel_assignment_control{UserDefined, Call}

				update_modwheel_assignment_circles{UserDefined, Call}

		end if
	end if
end on

function wait_or_zero(wait_time : int){thread-unsafe}

		wait(wait_time{int}){Builtin, None}
	end if
end function

function ui_button_toggle_except(ui_array : int[], exception_idx : int, idx0 : int)
	idx0{int} := 0
	idx0{int} := 0
	while(idx0{int} <= (num_elements[ui_array{int[]}] - 1)) 
		if(idx0{int} # exception_idx{int})
			set_control_par(ui_array[idx0{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, OFF{int}){Builtin, None}
		else
			set_control_par(ui_array[idx0{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, ON{int}){Builtin, None}
		end if
		inc(idx0{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
end function

function subarticulation_event_set_event_id(subarticulation_event_id : int, event_id : int)
	subarticulation_event_list[subarticulation_event_id{int}]{int} := event_id{int}
end function

function subarticulation_octave_layer_set_event_id(subarticulation_event_id : int, event_id : int)
	subarticulation_event_octave_layer_id[subarticulation_event_id{int}]{int} := event_id{int}
end function

function subarticulation_event_get_free_index(ret9 : int, idx5 : int, result5 : int)
	idx5{int} := 0
	result5{int} := - 1
	idx5{int} := 0
	while(idx5{int} < MAX_SUBARTICULATION_EVENTS{int}) 
		if((subarticulation_event_list[idx5{int}]{int} = - 1) and (subarticulation_event_last_used[idx5{int}]{int} < (ENGINE_UPTIME{int} - lookahead{int})))
			result5{int} := idx5{int}
			idx5{int} := MAX_SUBARTICULATION_EVENTS{int}
		end if
		idx5{int} := idx5{int} + 1
	end while

function subarticulation_group_count(ret0 : int, subarticulation_id : int, group_count0 : int)

	if(subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{int}]{int}]{int} = SUBARTICULATION_TYPE_LEGATO{int})
		group_count0{int} := NUM_MIC_POSITIONS{int} * ((subarticulations_dynamic_layers[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{int}]{int}]{int} * 3) + subarticulations_trans_num[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{int}]{int}]{int})

	end if
	ret0{int} := group_count0{int}
end function

function articulation_event_get_free_index(ret1 : int, next_free_idx0 : int, idx3 : int, i1 : int, is_free0 : int, _ret110 : int, result10 : int)

		is_free0{int} := TRUE{int}
		i1{int} := 0
		while(i1{int} <= (4 - 1)) 
			if(_articulation_event_list[(idx3{int} * 4) + i1{int}]{int} # - 1)
				is_free0{int} := FALSE{int}
			end if
			inc(i1{int}){Builtin, None}
		end while
			_ret110{int} := 0
				event_list_contains(_ret110{int}, idx3{int}, result10{int}){UserDefined, ParameterStack}

			if((is_free0{int} = TRUE{int}) and (_ret110{int} = FALSE{int}))
				next_free_idx0{int} := idx3{int}
			end if

		idx3{int} := idx3{int} + 1
	end while
	if(next_free_idx0{int} = - 1)
		message("Articulation Event Buffer Full"){Builtin, None}
	end if
	ret1{int} := next_free_idx0{int}
end function

function articulations_note_off(instrument_slot : int, note : int, ks1 : int, i3 : int, _ret90 : int, result20 : int, result21 : int)
	ks1{int} := 0
	i3{int} := 0

			_ret90{int} := 0
				event_list_get_articulation_event(_ret90{int}, instrument_slot{int}, ks1{int}, note{int}, result20{int}){UserDefined, ParameterStack}

			if(_ret90{int} # - 1)
				i3{int} := 0
				while(i3{int} <= (4 - 1)) 
					if(_loaded_subarticulations[(instrument_slot{int} * 32) + ((ks1{int} * 4) + i3{int})]{int} # - 1)
							result20{int} := 0
								event_list_get_articulation_event(result20{int}, instrument_slot{int}, ks1{int}, note{int}, result21{int}){UserDefined, ParameterStack}

								delay_buffer_add(result20{int}, instrument_slot{int}, ks1{int}, i3{int}, note{int}, - 1, 0, ENGINE_UPTIME{int}, lookahead{int} - subarticulations_start_offset[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[(instrument_slot{int} * 32) + ((ks1{int} * 4) + i3{int})]{int}]{int}]{int}, - 1, result21{int}){UserDefined, ParameterStack}


					end if
					inc(i3{int}){Builtin, None}
				end while
					event_list_remove_articulation_event(instrument_slot{int}, ks1{int}, note{int}){UserDefined, ParameterStack}

			end if

		inc(ks1{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
end function

function articulations_compute_level(ret6 : int, instrument_slot : int, keyswitch : int, note : int, subarticulation : int, subarticulation_modulation_strength0 : real, fade_in_start0 : int, fade_in_range0 : int, fade_out_end0 : int, fade_out_range0 : int)
	subarticulation_modulation_strength0{real} := 0
	fade_in_start0{int} := _loaded_subarticulations_start[(instrument_slot{int} * 32) + ((keyswitch{int} * 4) + subarticulation{int})]{int}
	fade_in_range0{int} := _loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[(instrument_slot{int} * 32) + ((keyswitch{int} * 4) + subarticulation{int})]{int}
	fade_out_end0{int} := _loaded_subarticulations_end[(instrument_slot{int} * 32) + ((keyswitch{int} * 4) + subarticulation{int})]{int}
	fade_out_range0{int} := _loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[(instrument_slot{int} * 32) + ((keyswitch{int} * 4) + subarticulation{int})]{int}
	if(in_range(modulation_positions[note{int} * use_polyphonic_modulation{int}]{int}, fade_in_start0{int}, fade_out_end0{int}){Builtin, None})
		subarticulation_modulation_strength0{real} := 1
		if(in_range(modulation_positions[note{int} * use_polyphonic_modulation{int}]{int}, fade_in_start0{int}, fade_in_start0{int} + fade_in_range0{int}){Builtin, None} and (fade_in_range0{int} > 0))
			subarticulation_modulation_strength0{real} := real(modulation_positions[note{int} * use_polyphonic_modulation{int}]{int} - fade_in_start0{int}){Builtin, None} / real(fade_in_range0{int}){Builtin, None}
		else
			if(in_range(modulation_positions[note{int} * use_polyphonic_modulation{int}]{int}, fade_out_end0{int} - fade_out_range0{int}, fade_out_end0{int}){Builtin, None} and (fade_out_range0{int} > 0))
				subarticulation_modulation_strength0{real} := real(fade_out_end0{int} - modulation_positions[note{int} * use_polyphonic_modulation{int}]{int}){Builtin, None} / real(fade_out_range0{int}){Builtin, None}
			end if
		end if
	end if
	ret6{int} := int(1e+06 * ((real(int(round(real(_articulation_volume_min[(instrument_slot{int} * 8) + keyswitch{int}]{int}){Builtin, None} + (real(_articulation_volume_max[(instrument_slot{int} * 8) + keyswitch{int}]{int} - _articulation_volume_min[(instrument_slot{int} * 8) + keyswitch{int}]{int}){Builtin, None} * pow(real(modulation_positions[note{int} * use_polyphonic_modulation{int}]{int}){Builtin, None} / 127, (real(_articulation_volume_curve[(instrument_slot{int} * 8) + keyswitch{int}]{int}){Builtin, None} / 100) + 1){Builtin, None})){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None} / 127) * subarticulation_modulation_strength0{real})){Builtin, None}
end function

function event_list_get_articulation_event(ret3 : int, instrument_slot : int, keyswitch : int, note : int, result2 : int)
	result2{int} := - 1
	if((((((instrument_slot{int} >= 0) and (instrument_slot{int} < NUM_INSTRUMENTS{int})) and (keyswitch{int} >= 0)) and (keyswitch{int} < NUM_KEYSWITCHES{int})) and (note{int} >= 0)) and (note{int} < 128))
		result2{int} := _event_list[(instrument_slot{int} * 1024) + ((keyswitch{int} * 128) + note{int})]{int}
	end if
	ret3{int} := result2{int}
end function

function event_list_remove_articulation_event(instrument_slot : int, keyswitch : int, note : int)
	if(((instrument_slot{int} # - 1) and (keyswitch{int} # - 1)) and (note{int} # - 1))
		if(_event_list[(instrument_slot{int} * 1024) + ((keyswitch{int} * 128) + note{int})]{int} >= 0)
			_event_list[(instrument_slot{int} * 1024) + ((keyswitch{int} * 128) + note{int})]{int} := - 1
		end if
	end if
end function

function event_list_add_articulation_event(instrument_slot : int, keyswitch : int, note : int, event : int)
	_event_list[(instrument_slot{int} * 1024) + ((keyswitch{int} * 128) + note{int})]{int} := event{int}
	articulation_event_instrument[event{int}]{int} := instrument_slot{int}
	articulation_event_keyswitch[event{int}]{int} := keyswitch{int}
	articulation_event_note[event{int}]{int} := note{int}
end function

function event_list_contains(ret2 : int, articulation_id : int, result1 : int)
	result1{int} := FALSE{int}
	if(search[_event_list{int[]}, articulation_id{int}] # - 1)
		result1{int} := TRUE{int}
	end if
	ret2{int} := result1{int}
end function

function delay_buffer_add(articulation_id : int, instrument : int, keyswitch : int, subarticulation : int, note : int, velo : int, interval : int, time : int, countdown : int, previous_note : int, idx4 : int)
	idx4{int} := search[delay_buffer{int[]}, - 1]
	if(idx4{int} # - 1)
		delay_buffer[idx4{int}]{int} := articulation_id{int}
		delay_buffer_instrument[idx4{int}]{int} := instrument{int}
		delay_buffer_keyswitch[idx4{int}]{int} := keyswitch{int}
		delay_buffer_subarticulation[idx4{int}]{int} := subarticulation{int}
		delay_buffer_note[idx4{int}]{int} := note{int}
		delay_buffer_velo[idx4{int}]{int} := velo{int}
		delay_buffer_interval[idx4{int}]{int} := interval{int}
		delay_buffer_time[idx4{int}]{int} := time{int}
		delay_buffer_countdown[idx4{int}]{int} := countdown{int}
		delay_buffer_prev_note[idx4{int}]{int} := previous_note{int}
		any_delay_event_queued{int} := TRUE{int}
	else
		message("WARNING: Delay Buffer Full"){Builtin, None}
	end if
end function

function update_selected_notes(ks2 : int, result00 : int, i20 : int, articulation_event_id00 : int, set_articulation_event_id00 : int, next_free_idx000 : int, idx300 : int, i100 : int, is_free000 : int, _ret11000 : int, result1000 : int)
	ks2{int} := 0
	pressed_key_idx{int} := 0
	i{int} := 0
	while(i{int} <= 127) 
		if(pressed_keys[i{int}]{int} > (ENGINE_UPTIME{int} - input_acceptance_time{int}))
			inst{int} := 0
			while(inst{int} <= (NUM_INSTRUMENTS{int} - 1)) 
					is_in_note_selection(pressed_key_idx{int}, num_pressed_keys{int}, note_selections[inst{int}]{int}, result00{int}){UserDefined, ParameterStack}

				if(is_in_note_selection_boolean{int} = TRUE{int})
					message("notens " & i{int}){Builtin, None}
						articulations_on_note(inst{int}, i{int}, key_velocity[i{int}]{int}, pressed_keys[i{int}]{int} - ENGINE_UPTIME{int}, result00{int}, i20{int}, articulation_event_id00{int}, set_articulation_event_id00{int}, next_free_idx000{int}, idx300{int}, i100{int}, is_free000{int}, _ret11000{int}, result1000{int}){UserDefined, ParameterStack}

				else
					ks2{int} := 0
					while(ks2{int} < NUM_KEYSWITCHES{int}) 
							result00{int} := 0
								event_list_get_articulation_event(result00{int}, inst{int}, ks2{int}, i{int}, i20{int}){UserDefined, ParameterStack}

							if(result00{int} # - 1)
									articulations_note_off(inst{int}, i{int}, i20{int}, idx300{int}, _ret11000{int}, articulation_event_id00{int}, i100{int}){UserDefined, ParameterStack}

								ks2{int} := NUM_KEYSWITCHES{int}
							end if

						inc(ks2{int}){Builtin, None}
					end while
				end if
				inc(inst{int}){Builtin, None}
			end while
		else
			if(pressed_keys[i{int}]{int} > 0)
				inst{int} := 0
				while(inst{int} <= (NUM_INSTRUMENTS{int} - 1)) 
						is_in_note_selection(pressed_key_idx{int}, num_pressed_keys{int}, note_selections[inst{int}]{int}, result00{int}){UserDefined, ParameterStack}

					if(is_in_note_selection_boolean{int} = FALSE{int})
							articulations_note_off(inst{int}, i{int}, result00{int}, i100{int}, articulation_event_id00{int}, _ret11000{int}, idx300{int}){UserDefined, ParameterStack}

					end if
					inc(inst{int}){Builtin, None}
				end while
			end if
		end if
		if(pressed_keys[i{int}]{int} > 0)
			inc(pressed_key_idx{int}){Builtin, None}
		end if
		inc(i{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
end function

function get_next_rr(ret7 : int, instrument : int, keyswitch : int, subarticulation_idx : int, note : int, rr0 : int)
	rr0{int} := 0
	if(subarticulations_rrr[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[(instrument{int} * 32) + ((keyswitch{int} * 4) + subarticulation_idx{int})]{int}]{int}]{int} = 0)
		rr0{int} := (_rr_data_idx[(instrument{int} * 4096) + ((keyswitch{int} * 512) + ((subarticulation_idx{int} * 128) + note{int}))]{int} + 1) mod subarticulations_rr_num[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[(instrument{int} * 32) + ((keyswitch{int} * 4) + subarticulation_idx{int})]{int}]{int}]{int}
	else
		if((ENGINE_UPTIME{int} - _rr_data_time[(instrument{int} * 4096) + ((keyswitch{int} * 512) + ((subarticulation_idx{int} * 128) + note{int}))]{int}) > subarticulations_rrr_reset_time[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[(instrument{int} * 32) + ((keyswitch{int} * 4) + subarticulation_idx{int})]{int}]{int}]{int})
			rr0{int} := (_rr_data_idx[(instrument{int} * 4096) + ((keyswitch{int} * 512) + ((subarticulation_idx{int} * 128) + note{int}))]{int} + 1) mod subarticulations_rrr[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[(instrument{int} * 32) + ((keyswitch{int} * 4) + subarticulation_idx{int})]{int}]{int}]{int}
		else
			rr0{int} := subarticulations_rrr[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[(instrument{int} * 32) + ((keyswitch{int} * 4) + subarticulation_idx{int})]{int}]{int}]{int} - ((subarticulations_rrr[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[(instrument{int} * 32) + ((keyswitch{int} * 4) + subarticulation_idx{int})]{int}]{int}]{int} - ((_rr_data_idx[(instrument{int} * 4096) + ((keyswitch{int} * 512) + ((subarticulation_idx{int} * 128) + note{int}))]{int} + 1) mod subarticulations_rr_num[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[(instrument{int} * 32) + ((keyswitch{int} * 4) + subarticulation_idx{int})]{int}]{int}]{int})) .and. sh_right(subarticulations_rrr[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[(instrument{int} * 32) + ((keyswitch{int} * 4) + subarticulation_idx{int})]{int}]{int}]{int} - ((_rr_data_idx[(instrument{int} * 4096) + ((keyswitch{int} * 512) + ((subarticulation_idx{int} * 128) + note{int}))]{int} + 1) mod subarticulations_rr_num[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[(instrument{int} * 32) + ((keyswitch{int} * 4) + subarticulation_idx{int})]{int}]{int}]{int}), 31){Builtin, None})
		end if
		_rr_data_time[(instrument{int} * 4096) + ((keyswitch{int} * 512) + ((subarticulation_idx{int} * 128) + note{int}))]{int} := ENGINE_UPTIME{int}
	end if
	_rr_data_idx[(instrument{int} * 4096) + ((keyswitch{int} * 512) + ((subarticulation_idx{int} * 128) + note{int}))]{int} := rr0{int}
	ret7{int} := rr0{int}
end function

function get_legato_data(ret10 : int, _legato_data_array : int[], instrument : int, subarticulation_idx : int, note : int, layer : int, transition : int, result6 : int)
	result6{int} := - 1
	if((((((((instrument{int} >= 0) and (instrument{int} < NUM_INSTRUMENTS{int})) and (subarticulation_idx{int} >= 0)) and (subarticulation_idx{int} < 4)) and (note{int} >= 0)) and (note{int} < 128)) and (layer{int} >= 0)) and (layer{int} < MAX_TRANSITION_DYN_LAYERS{int}))
		if((transition{int} >= 0) and (transition{int} < MAX_TRANSITIONS_PER_NOTE{int}))
			result6{int} := _legato_data_array[(instrument{int} * (((num_elements[_legato_data_array{int[]}, 2] * num_elements[_legato_data_array{int[]}, 3]) * num_elements[_legato_data_array{int[]}, 4]) * num_elements[_legato_data_array{int[]}, 5])) + ((subarticulation_idx{int} * ((num_elements[_legato_data_array{int[]}, 3] * num_elements[_legato_data_array{int[]}, 4]) * num_elements[_legato_data_array{int[]}, 5])) + ((layer{int} * (num_elements[_legato_data_array{int[]}, 4] * num_elements[_legato_data_array{int[]}, 5])) + ((note{int} * num_elements[_legato_data_array{int[]}, 5]) + transition{int})))]{int}
		else
			if(transition{int} = - 1)
				result6{int} := _legato_data_array[(instrument{int} * (((num_elements[_legato_data_array{int[]}, 2] * num_elements[_legato_data_array{int[]}, 3]) * num_elements[_legato_data_array{int[]}, 4]) * num_elements[_legato_data_array{int[]}, 5])) + ((subarticulation_idx{int} * ((num_elements[_legato_data_array{int[]}, 3] * num_elements[_legato_data_array{int[]}, 4]) * num_elements[_legato_data_array{int[]}, 5])) + (layer{int} * (num_elements[_legato_data_array{int[]}, 4] * num_elements[_legato_data_array{int[]}, 5])))]{int}
			end if
		end if
	end if
	ret10{int} := result6{int}
end function

		end if
		inc(i0{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
end function

function update_keyswitch_volume_curve
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_min{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, _articulation_volume_min[(selected_instrument{int} * 8) + selected_keyswitch{int}]{int}){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_max{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, _articulation_volume_max[(selected_instrument{int} * 8) + selected_keyswitch{int}]{int}){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(sli_keyswitch_volume_curve{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, _articulation_volume_curve[(selected_instrument{int} * 8) + selected_keyswitch{int}]{int} * - 1){Builtin, None}
	i{int} := 0
	while(i{int} <= (num_elements[lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope{int[]}] - 1)) 
		set_control_par(lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT{int}, int(round(real(int((real(_articulation_volume_min[(selected_instrument{int} * 8) + selected_keyswitch{int}]{int}){Builtin, None} / 127) * 30){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None} + (real(int((real(_articulation_volume_max[(selected_instrument{int} * 8) + selected_keyswitch{int}]{int}){Builtin, None} / 127) * 30){Builtin, None} - int((real(_articulation_volume_min[(selected_instrument{int} * 8) + selected_keyswitch{int}]{int}){Builtin, None} / 127) * 30){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None} * pow(real(i{int}){Builtin, None} / real(num_elements[lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope{int[]}]){Builtin, None}, (real(_articulation_volume_curve[(selected_instrument{int} * 8) + selected_keyswitch{int}]{int}){Builtin, None} / 100) + 1){Builtin, None})){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
		set_control_par(lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y{int}, get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_line{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y{int}){Builtin, None} - get_control_par(lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT{int}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
		inc(i{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
end function

function update_modwheel_assignment_control
	xy_modwheel_assignment[2]{real} := real(_loaded_subarticulations_start[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int}){Builtin, None} / 127
	xy_modwheel_assignment[0]{real} := real(_loaded_subarticulations_start[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int} + _loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int}){Builtin, None} / 127
	xy_modwheel_assignment[4]{real} := real(_loaded_subarticulations_end[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int} - _loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int}){Builtin, None} / 127
	xy_modwheel_assignment[6]{real} := real(_loaded_subarticulations_end[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int}){Builtin, None} / 127
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_modwheel_assignment_left{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}, get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None} + int(xy_modwheel_assignment[2]{real} * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH{int}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_in{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}, get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_modwheel_assignment_left{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None} + int(- 200 + ((xy_modwheel_assignment[0]{real} - xy_modwheel_assignment[2]{real}) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH{int}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None})){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_in{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE{int}, int((xy_modwheel_assignment[0]{real} - xy_modwheel_assignment[2]{real}) * 200){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_modwheel_assignment_constant{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}, get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_modwheel_assignment_left{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None} + int(round((xy_modwheel_assignment[0]{real} - xy_modwheel_assignment[2]{real}) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH{int}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_modwheel_assignment_constant{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH{int}, int((xy_modwheel_assignment[4]{real} - xy_modwheel_assignment[0]{real}) * 200){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_out{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}, get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None} + int(xy_modwheel_assignment[4]{real} * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH{int}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_out{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE{int}, int((xy_modwheel_assignment[6]{real} - xy_modwheel_assignment[4]{real}) * 200){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_modwheel_assignment_right{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}, get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None} + int(xy_modwheel_assignment[6]{real} * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH{int}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
end function

function update_modwheel_assignment_cursor(modwheel : int)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_modwheel_assignment_cursor{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}, (get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None} - 5) + int(real(get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH{int}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None} * (real(modwheel{int}){Builtin, None} / 127)){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
end function

function update_modwheel_assignment_circles
	i{int} := 0
	while(i{int} <= (4 - 1)) 
		set_control_par(lbl_center_circle[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{int}){Builtin, None}
		set_control_par(lbl_center_circle_bound_left[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{int}){Builtin, None}
		set_control_par(lbl_center_circle_bound_right[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{int}){Builtin, None}
		if(_loaded_subarticulations[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + i{int})]{int} # - 1)
			set_control_par(lbl_center_circle[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int}){Builtin, None}
			set_control_par(lbl_center_circle_bound_left[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int}){Builtin, None}
			set_control_par(lbl_center_circle_bound_right[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int}){Builtin, None}
			if(i{int} = selected_subarticulation{int})
				set_control_par_str(lbl_center_circle[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE{int}, "modwheel-circle-selected-" & i{int}){Builtin, None}
				set_control_par_str(lbl_center_circle_bound_left[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE{int}, "modwheel-circle-handle-left-" & i{int}){Builtin, None}
				set_control_par_str(lbl_center_circle_bound_right[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE{int}, "modwheel-circle-handle-right-" & i{int}){Builtin, None}
			else
				set_control_par_str(lbl_center_circle[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE{int}, "modwheel-circle-unselected-" & i{int}){Builtin, None}
				set_control_par_str(lbl_center_circle_bound_left[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE{int}, "modwheel-circle-darken-left-" & i{int}){Builtin, None}
				set_control_par_str(lbl_center_circle_bound_right[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE{int}, "modwheel-circle-darken-right-" & i{int}){Builtin, None}
			end if
			set_control_par(lbl_center_circle_bound_left[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE{int}, _loaded_subarticulations_start[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + i{int})]{int}){Builtin, None}
			set_control_par(lbl_center_circle_bound_right[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE{int}, 127 - _loaded_subarticulations_end[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + i{int})]{int}){Builtin, None}
		end if
		inc(i{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
end function

function update_circle_modwheel_position(modwheel : int)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_center_circle_indicator{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE{int}, modwheel{int} - 1){Builtin, None}
end function

function update_dynamic_range_control
	xy_dynamic_range[0]{real} := real(_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_lower[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int}){Builtin, None} / 127
	xy_dynamic_range[2]{real} := real(_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_upper[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int}){Builtin, None} / 127
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}, get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None} + int(xy_dynamic_range[0]{real} * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH{int}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}, get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None} + int(xy_dynamic_range[2]{real} * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH{int}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_line{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}, get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_line{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH{int}, get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None} - get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
		update_dynamic_range_cursor(modulation_positions[0 * use_polyphonic_modulation{int}]{int}){UserDefined, Inlining}

end function

function update_dynamic_range_cursor(modwheel : int)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_cursor{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}, (get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None} - 5) + int((real(((modwheel{int} * (1 + (sh_right(127 - modwheel{int}, 31){Builtin, None} .or. sh_right(modwheel{int} - 1, 31){Builtin, None}))) - (1 * sh_right(modwheel{int} - 1, 31){Builtin, None})) - (127 * sh_right(127 - modwheel{int}, 31){Builtin, None})){Builtin, None} / 127) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None} - get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
end function

function editor_update_modwheel_position(modwheel : int)
		update_dynamic_range_cursor(modwheel{int}){UserDefined, ParameterStack}

		update_circle_modwheel_position(modwheel{int}){UserDefined, ParameterStack}

		update_modwheel_assignment_cursor(modwheel{int}){UserDefined, ParameterStack}

		update_keyswitch_volume_curve_cursor(modwheel{int}){UserDefined, ParameterStack}

end function

function center_circle_distance(ret11 : real, x : real, y : real, dx0 : real, dy0 : real)
	dx0{real} := x{real} - 0.5
	dy0{real} := y{real} - 0.5
	ret11{real} := sqrt((dx0{real} * dx0{real}) + (dy0{real} * dy0{real})){Builtin, None}
end function

function center_circle_angle(ret12 : real, x : real, y : real, dx1 : real, dy1 : real, cos_theta0 : real, angle0 : real)
	dx1{real} := x{real} - 0.5
	dy1{real} := y{real} - 0.5
	cos_theta0{real} := dx1{real} / sqrt((dx1{real} * dx1{real}) + (dy1{real} * dy1{real})){Builtin, None}
	angle0{real} := acos(cos_theta0{real}){Builtin, None}
	if(dy1{real} < 0)
		angle0{real} := (2 * NI_MATH_PI{real}) - angle0{real}
	end if
	ret12{real} := angle0{real}
end function

function angle_to_value(ret13 : int, angle : real, angle_min : real, angle_max : real, new_angle0 : real)
	new_angle0{real} := angle{real} + (NI_MATH_PI{real} / 2)
	if(new_angle0{real} > (NI_MATH_PI{real} * 2))
		new_angle0{real} := new_angle0{real} - (2 * NI_MATH_PI{real})
	end if
	new_angle0{real} := abs(new_angle0{real} - (2 * NI_MATH_PI{real})){Builtin, None}
	ret13{int} := int((127 * (new_angle0{real} - angle_min{real})) / (angle_max{real} - angle_min{real})){Builtin, None}
end function

	if(idx7{int} # - 1)
		set_engine_par(ENGINE_PAR_VOLUME{int}, get_control_par(sli_mixer_channel_volume[idx7{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}){Builtin, None}, - 1, - 1, NI_BUS_OFFSET{int} + idx7{int}){Builtin, None}
	end if
end function

function show_keyswitches(const bool : int)
	if(bool{int} = TRUE{int})
		set_control_par(get_ui_id(pnl_keyswitches{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int}){Builtin, None}
	else
		set_control_par(get_ui_id(pnl_keyswitches{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{int}){Builtin, None}
	end if
end function

function swi_keyswitch_ui_controls(uiid : int, idx6 : int, idx00001 : int)
	idx6{int} := search[swi_keyswitch{int[]}, uiid{int}]
	if(idx6{int} # - 1)
		if(get_control_par(swi_keyswitch[idx6{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_KEY_SHIFT{int}){Builtin, None} = OFF{int})
			i{int} := 0
			while(i{int} <= (NUM_KEYSWITCHES{int} - 1)) 
				_keyswitch_states[(selected_instrument{int} * 8) + i{int}]{int} := OFF{int}
				inc(i{int}){Builtin, None}
			end while
		end if
		_keyswitch_states[(selected_instrument{int} * 8) + idx6{int}]{int} := ON{int}
		selected_keyswitch{int} := idx6{int}
			update_keyswitch_selection(idx00001{int}){UserDefined, ParameterStack}

	end if
end function

function update_keyswitch_selection(idx0000 : int)
	i{int} := 0
	while(i{int} <= (NUM_KEYSWITCHES{int} - 1)) 
		set_control_par(swi_keyswitch[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, _keyswitch_states[(selected_instrument{int} * 8) + i{int}]{int}){Builtin, None}
		set_control_par_str(swi_keyswitch[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXT{int}, _articulation_names[(selected_instrument{int} * 8) + i{int}]{string}){Builtin, None}
		set_key_pressed((keyswitch_octave{int} * 12) + i{int}, _keyswitch_states[(selected_instrument{int} * 8) + i{int}]{int}){Builtin, None}
		inc(i{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
		keyswitches_color_keys{UserDefined, Inlining}

	if(get_control_par(get_ui_id(pnl_editor_page{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}){Builtin, None} = HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int})
			editor_page_open(idx0000{int}){UserDefined, Inlining}

	end if
end function

function keyswitches_color_keys
	i{int} := 0
	while(i{int} <= (NUM_KEYSWITCHES{int} - 1)) 
		set_key_color((keyswitch_octave{int} * 12) + i{int}, KEY_COLOR_RED{int}){Builtin, None}
		if(_keyswitch_states[(selected_instrument{int} * 8) + i{int}]{int} = ON{int})
			set_key_color((keyswitch_octave{int} * 12) + i{int}, KEY_COLOR_ORANGE{int}){Builtin, None}
		end if
		inc(i{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
end function

function keyswitches_on_note(note : int, check_before0 : int, changed0 : int, idx00000 : int)
	check_before0{int} := 0
	changed0{int} := FALSE{int}
	if(in_range(note{int}, keyswitch_octave{int} * 12, ((keyswitch_octave{int} * 12) + NUM_KEYSWITCHES{int}) - 1){Builtin, None})
		i{int} := 0
		while(i{int} <= (NUM_KEYSWITCHES{int} - 1)) 
			check_before0{int} := _keyswitch_states[(selected_instrument{int} * 8) + i{int}]{int}
			_keyswitch_states[(selected_instrument{int} * 8) + i{int}]{int} := KEY_DOWN[(keyswitch_octave{int} * 12) + i{int}]{int}
			if(check_before0{int} # _keyswitch_states[(selected_instrument{int} * 8) + i{int}]{int})
				changed0{int} := TRUE{int}
			end if
			inc(i{int}){Builtin, None}
		end while
		if(changed0{int} = TRUE{int})
				update_keyswitch_selection(idx00000{int}){UserDefined, ParameterStack}

		end if
	end if
end function

	end while
end function

function find_loaded_legato
	authoring_page_active{int} := FALSE{int}
	if(_loaded_subarticulations[0]{int} # - 1)
		if(subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[0]{int}]{int}]{int} = SUBARTICULATION_TYPE_LEGATO{int})
			authoring_page_active{int} := TRUE{int}
			set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_authoring_legato_title{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXT{int}, subarticulations_full_name[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[0]{int}]{int}]{string} & " (" & _loaded_subarticulations[0]{int} & ")"){Builtin, None}
		end if
	end if
end function

function update_authoring_transition(start_note : int, end_note : int, dynamic_layer : int)
	if(get_control_par(get_ui_id(btn_authoring_follow{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}){Builtin, None} = ON{int})
		set_control_par(get_ui_id(vlue_authoring_start_note{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, start_note{int}){Builtin, None}
		set_control_par(get_ui_id(vlue_authoring_end_note{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, end_note{int}){Builtin, None}
		set_control_par(get_ui_id(mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, dynamic_layer{int}){Builtin, None}
		if(abs(start_note{int} - end_note{int}){Builtin, None} <= 12)
			authoring_interval_valid{int} := TRUE{int}
			set_control_par(get_ui_id(sli_sustain_release{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, _legato_data_sus_release_time[(mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer{int} * 3200) + ((start_note{int} * 25) + (abs(end_note{int} - start_note{int}){Builtin, None} + (- sh_right(- (end_note{int} - start_note{int}), 31){Builtin, None} * 12)))]{int}){Builtin, None}
			set_control_par(get_ui_id(sli_trans_start{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, _legato_data_trans_zone_start[(mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer{int} * 3200) + ((start_note{int} * 25) + (abs(end_note{int} - start_note{int}){Builtin, None} + (- sh_right(- (end_note{int} - start_note{int}), 31){Builtin, None} * 12)))]{int}){Builtin, None}
			set_control_par(get_ui_id(sli_trans_fadeIn{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, _legato_data_trans_fade_in_time[(mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer{int} * 3200) + ((start_note{int} * 25) + (abs(end_note{int} - start_note{int}){Builtin, None} + (- sh_right(- (end_note{int} - start_note{int}), 31){Builtin, None} * 12)))]{int}){Builtin, None}
			set_control_par(get_ui_id(sli_trans_volume{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, _legato_data_trans_zone_volume[(mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer{int} * 3200) + ((start_note{int} * 25) + (abs(end_note{int} - start_note{int}){Builtin, None} + (- sh_right(- (end_note{int} - start_note{int}), 31){Builtin, None} * 12)))]{int}){Builtin, None}
			set_control_par(get_ui_id(sli_trans_fadeOut{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, _legato_data_trans_fade_out_time[(mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer{int} * 3200) + ((start_note{int} * 25) + (abs(end_note{int} - start_note{int}){Builtin, None} + (- sh_right(- (end_note{int} - start_note{int}), 31){Builtin, None} * 12)))]{int}){Builtin, None}
			set_control_par(get_ui_id(sli_sustain_wait{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, _legato_data_sus_wait_time[(mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer{int} * 3200) + ((start_note{int} * 25) + (abs(end_note{int} - start_note{int}){Builtin, None} + (- sh_right(- (end_note{int} - start_note{int}), 31){Builtin, None} * 12)))]{int}){Builtin, None}
			set_control_par(get_ui_id(sli_sustain_fadeIn{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, _legato_data_sus_fade_in_time[(mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer{int} * 3200) + ((start_note{int} * 25) + (abs(end_note{int} - start_note{int}){Builtin, None} + (- sh_right(- (end_note{int} - start_note{int}), 31){Builtin, None} * 12)))]{int}){Builtin, None}
				update_authoring_labels{UserDefined, Call}

		else
			authoring_interval_valid{int} := FALSE{int}
		end if
	end if
end function

function update_authoring_labels
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_sustain_release{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXT{int}, sli_sustain_release{int} & " ms"){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_trans_start{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXT{int}, int((real(sli_trans_start{int}){Builtin, None} / 1e+06) * 750){Builtin, None} & " ms"){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_trans_fadeIn{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXT{int}, int((real(sli_trans_fadeIn{int}){Builtin, None} / 1e+06) * 750){Builtin, None} & " ms"){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_trans_volume{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXT{int}, (round((real(sli_trans_volume{int}){Builtin, None} / 1000) * pow(10, int_to_real(2){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None} / pow(10, int_to_real(2){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}) & " dB"){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_trans_fadeOut{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXT{int}, int((real(sli_trans_fadeOut{int}){Builtin, None} / 1e+06) * 1000){Builtin, None} & " ms"){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_sustain_wait{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXT{int}, int((real(sli_sustain_wait{int}){Builtin, None} / 1e+06) * 500){Builtin, None} & " ms"){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_sustain_fadeIn{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXT{int}, int((real(sli_sustain_fadeIn{int}){Builtin, None} / 1e+06) * 500){Builtin, None} & " ms"){Builtin, None}
end function

function credits_open
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(pnl_credits{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int}){Builtin, None}
end function

function credits_close
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(pnl_credits{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{int}){Builtin, None}
end function

function Array::clip(x : int, b : int)
	return (x{int} + ((- x{int} .and. sh_right(x{int}, 31){Builtin, None}) + ((x{int} - b{int}) .and. sh_right(b{int} - x{int}, 31){Builtin, None})))
end function
